charge seruant learne meaning old prouerbe hard matter make bed dogge man cannot tell side hee lye goeth turning round ready lye downe seruant cannot tell seruice may acceptable agreable maister hart variable diuers therefore maister delicate nature hee muste determyne wyth hymselfe take anye payne seruice yet scarse ynough contene must take heed falling common errour seruauntes like new broome whiche sweepeth house cleane serue diligentlye first growe slouthfull waye gette fauour hee beginneth wel worthy recompense perseuereth wel seruaunt must thinke mayster looke rather heate coole
